\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00522}00522         numRows = height * 2; \textcolor{comment}{// Direct3D makes this simplifying assumption, although it is larger than the 4:1:1 data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00523}00523         numBytes = rowBytes * numRows;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00524}00524     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00525}00525     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (planar)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00526}00526     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00527}00527         rowBytes = ( ( width + 1 ) >> 1 ) * bpe;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00528}00528         numBytes = ( rowBytes * height ) + ( ( rowBytes * height + 1 ) >> 1 );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00529}00529         numRows = height + ( ( height + 1 ) >> 1 );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00530}00530     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00531}00531     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00533}00533         \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} bpp = BitsPerPixel( fmt );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00534}00534         rowBytes = ( width * bpp + 7 ) / 8; \textcolor{comment}{// round up to nearest byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00535}00535         numRows = height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00536}00536         numBytes = rowBytes * height;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00537}00537     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_d_d_s_texture_loader_8cpp_source_l00538}00538 }
